I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
BUG: 'setup-cli' action referenced by mutable tag instead of commit SHA in maintenance workflow
## Summary

The `agentics-maintenance.yml` workflow compiled by gh-aw v0.64.0 references `github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli` using the mutable tag `@v0.64.0` rather than a pinned full commit SHA. Every other action in this repo (and in `copilot-setup-steps.yml`) is pinned to a commit SHA for supply-chain integrity and reproducibility. This inconsistency weakens the security posture of the workflow.

### What failed
- `uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@v0.64.0` — mutable tag, not a SHA pin.
- All other action references in the same repository use SHA-pinned references.

### Why it failed
- The compiler's action pinning logic (via `GetActionPin()` and `.github/aw/actions-lock.json`) did not resolve and emit the commit SHA for `setup-cli` in the context of the maintenance workflow generation.

### Root cause
- Gap in the action pinning/lock resolution logic in the compiler when generating maintenance workflow references to `setup-cli`.
- The correct SHA is known (`51c65948c64ab6752536ead71fba1fc2c20ed0bc`) and is used elsewhere; it simply wasn't applied here.

### Supporting evidence / References
- [PR Review Copilot observation 11](https://github.com/grahame-org/gnu-tools-for-stm32/pull/682#pullrequestreview-4013076953)
- Compiler pinning code: `GetActionPin()` and `.github/aw/actions-lock.json`
- Example of correct SHA pinning in `copilot-setup-steps.yml` in same repo

### Proposed fix
- Ensure `GetActionPin()` (or equivalent) correctly resolves and emits the SHA for `setup-cli` in all compiler code paths, including maintenance workflow generation.
- The suggestion from review: `uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@51c65948c64ab6752536ead71fba1fc2c20ed0bc # v0.64.0`
- Add a compiler test asserting that all emitted action references are SHA-pinned (no bare tags).

### Implementation plan
1. Audit compiler workflow generators for any `setup-cli` or other action references that bypass the `GetActionPin()` / `actions-lock.json` resolution path.
2. Fix the identified code path to use the SHA from the lock.
3. Add a test asserting no mutable tag references in any compiled `.lock.yml` output.


</pr_description>

    23	// Example: "actions/checkout@abc123 # v4.1.0"
    24	func formatActionReference(repo, sha, version string) string {
    25	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s # %s", repo, sha, version)

    29	// Example: "actions/checkout@v4"
    30	func formatActionCacheKey(repo, version string) string {
    31	        return fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", repo, version)
    32	}

    34	// ActionPin represents a pinned GitHub Action with its commit SHA
    35	type ActionPin struct {
    36	        Repo    string                      `json:"repo"`             // e.g., "actions/checkout"
    37	        Version string                      `json:"version"`          // e.g., "v5" - the golden/default version
    38	        SHA     string                      `json:"sha"`              // Full commit SHA for the pinned version
    39	        Inputs  map[string]*ActionYAMLInput `json:"inputs,omitempty"` // optional cached inputs (not used for SHA pinning)
    40	}

    42	// ActionPinsData represents the structure of the embedded JSON file

    45	        Entries map[string]ActionPin `json:"entries"` // key: "repo@version"
    46	}

    48	var (

    50	        cachedActionPins []ActionPin
    51	        // actionPinsOnce ensures the action pins are loaded only once
    52	        actionPinsOnce sync.Once
    53	)
    54	
    55	// getActionPins returns the action pins from the embedded JSON
    56	// Returns a sorted slice of action pins (by version descending, then by repo name)
    57	// The data is parsed once on first call and cached for subsequent calls
    58	func getActionPins() []ActionPin {
    59	        actionPinsOnce.Do(func() {
    60	                actionPinsLog.Print("Unmarshaling action pins from embedded JSON (first call, will be cached)")
    61	
    62	                var data ActionPinsData
    63	                if err := json.Unmarshal(actionPinsJSON, &data); err != nil {
    64	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Failed to unmarshal action pins JSON: %v", err)
    65	                        panic(fmt.Sprintf("failed to load action pins: %v", err))
    66	                }
    67	
    68	                // Detect and log key/version mismatches
    69	                mismatchCount := 0
    70	                for key, pin := range data.Entries {
    71	                        // Extract version from key (format: "repo@version")
    72	                        if idx := strings.LastIndex(key, "@"); idx != -1 {
    73	                                keyVersion := key[idx+1:]
    74	                                if keyVersion != pin.Version {
    75	                                        mismatchCount++
    76	                                        // Safely truncate SHA for logging
    77	                                        shortSHA := pin.SHA
    78	                                        if len(pin.SHA) > 8 {
    79	                                                shortSHA = pin.SHA[:8]
    80	                                        }
    81	                                        actionPinsLog.Printf("WARNING: Key/version mismatch in action_pins.json: key=%s has version=%s but pin.Version=%s (sha=%s)",
    82	                                                key, keyVersion, pin.Version, shortSHA)
    83	                                }
    84	                        }
    85	                }
    86	                if mismatchCount > 0 {
    87	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Found %d key/version mismatches in action_pins.json", mismatchCount)
    88	                }
    89	
    90	                // Convert map values to slice - immutable initialization
    91	                pins := make([]ActionPin, 0, len(data.Entries))
    92	                for _, pin := range data.Entries {
    93	                        pins = append(pins, pin)
    94	                }
    95	
    96	                // Sort by version (descending) then by repo name (ascending)
    97	                // Use standard library sort for better performance O(n log n) vs O(n²)
    98	                sort.Slice(pins, func(i, j int) bool {
    99	                        // Compare versions first (descending order - higher version first)
   100	                        if pins[i].Version != pins[j].Version {
   101	                                return pins[i].Version > pins[j].Version
   102	                        }
   103	                        // Same version, sort by repo name (ascending order)
   104	                        return pins[i].Repo < pins[j].Repo
   105	                })
   106	
   107	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Successfully unmarshaled and sorted %d action pins from JSON", len(pins))
   108	                cachedActionPins = pins
   109	        })
   110	
   111	        return cachedActionPins
   112	}
   113	
   114	// sortPinsByVersion sorts action pins by version in descending order (highest first).
   115	// This function returns a new sorted slice without modifying the input.
   116	// This is an immutable operation for better safety and clarity.
   117	func sortPinsByVersion(pins []ActionPin) []ActionPin {
   118	        // Create a copy to avoid mutating the input
   119	        result := make([]ActionPin, len(pins))
   120	        copy(result, pins)
   121	
   122	        sort.Slice(result, func(i, j int) bool {
   123	                // Strip 'v' prefix for comparison
   124	                v1 := strings.TrimPrefix(result[i].Version, "v")
   125	                v2 := strings.TrimPrefix(result[j].Version, "v")
   126	                // Return true if v1 > v2 to get descending order
   127	                return compareVersions(v1, v2) > 0
   128	        })
   129	
   130	        return result
   131	}
   132	
   133	// GetActionPin returns the pinned action reference for a given action repository
   134	// When multiple versions exist for the same repo, it returns the latest version by semver
   135	// If no pin is found, it returns an empty string
   136	// The returned reference includes a comment with the version tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1")
   137	func GetActionPin(actionRepo string) string {
   138	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   139	
   140	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   141	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   142	                return pin.Repo == actionRepo
   143	        })
   144	
   145	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   146	                // If no pin exists, return empty string to signal that this action is not pinned
   147	                return ""
   148	        }
   149	
   150	        // Sort matching pins by version (descending - latest first) - immutable operation
   151	        sortedPins := sortPinsByVersion(matchingPins)
   152	
   153	        // Return the latest version (first after sorting)
   154	        latestPin := sortedPins[0]
   155	        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, latestPin.SHA, latestPin.Version)
   156	}
   157	
   158	// GetActionPinWithData returns the pinned action reference for a given action@version
   159	// It tries dynamic resolution first, then falls back to hardcoded pins
   160	// If resolution fails, emits a warning and returns empty string (in both strict and non-strict modes)
   161	// The returned reference includes a comment with the version tag (e.g., "repo@sha # v1")
   162	func GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, version string, data *WorkflowData) (string, error) {
   163	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Resolving action pin: repo=%s, version=%s, strict_mode=%t", actionRepo, version, data.StrictMode)
   164	
   165	        // Check if version is already a full 40-character SHA
   166	        isAlreadySHA := isValidFullSHA(version)
   167	
   168	        // First try dynamic resolution if resolver is available (but not for SHAs, as they can't be resolved)
   169	        if data.ActionResolver != nil && !isAlreadySHA {
   170	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Attempting dynamic resolution for %s@%s", actionRepo, version)
   171	                sha, err := data.ActionResolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, version)
   172	                if err == nil && sha != "" {
   173	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Dynamic resolution succeeded: %s@%s → %s", actionRepo, version, sha)
   174	
   175	                        // Successfully resolved - cache will be saved at end of compilation
   176	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Successfully resolved action pin (cache marked dirty, will save at end)")
   177	                        result := formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, version)
   178	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Returning pinned reference: %s", result)
   179	                        return result, nil
   180	                }
   181	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Dynamic resolution failed for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, version, err)
   182	        } else {
   183	                if isAlreadySHA {
   184	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Version is already a SHA, skipping dynamic resolution")
   185	                } else {
   186	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("No action resolver available, skipping dynamic resolution")
   187	                }
   188	        }
   189	
   190	        // Dynamic resolution failed, try hardcoded pins
   191	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Falling back to hardcoded pins for %s@%s", actionRepo, version)
   192	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   193	
   194	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   195	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   196	                return pin.Repo == actionRepo
   197	        })
   198	
   199	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   200	                // No pins found for this repo, will handle below
   201	                actionPinsLog.Printf("No hardcoded pins found for %s", actionRepo)
   202	        } else {
   203	                actionPinsLog.Printf("Found %d hardcoded pin(s) for %s", len(matchingPins), actionRepo)
   204	
   205	                // Sort matching pins by version (descending - highest first) - immutable operation
   206	                matchingPins = sortPinsByVersion(matchingPins)
   207	
   208	                // First, try to find an exact version match (for version tags)
   209	                for _, pin := range matchingPins {
   210	                        if pin.Version == version {
   211	                                actionPinsLog.Printf("Exact version match: requested=%s, found=%s", version, pin.Version)
   212	                                return formatActionReference(actionRepo, pin.SHA, pin.Version), nil
   213	                        }
   214	                }
   215	
   216	                // If version is a SHA, check if it matches any hardcoded pin's SHA
   217	                if isAlreadySHA {
   218	                        for _, pin := range matchingPins {
   219	                                if pin.SHA == version {
   220	                                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Exact SHA match: requested=%s, found version=%s", version, pin.Version)
   221	                                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, pin.SHA, pin.Version), nil
   222	                                }
   223	                        }
   224	                        // SHA provided but doesn't match any hardcoded pin - return it as-is without warnings
   225	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("SHA %s not found in hardcoded pins, returning as-is", version)
   226	                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, version, version), nil
   227	                }
   228	
   229	                // No exact match found
   230	                // In non-strict mode, find the highest semver-compatible version
   231	                // Semver compatibility means respecting major version boundaries
   232	                // (e.g., v5 -> highest v5.x.x, not v6.x.x)
   233	                if !data.StrictMode && len(matchingPins) > 0 {
   234	                        // Filter for semver-compatible pins (matching major version) - using functional filter
   235	                        compatiblePins := sliceutil.Filter(matchingPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   236	                                return isSemverCompatible(pin.Version, version)
   237	                        })
   238	
   239	                        // If we found compatible pins, use the highest one (first after sorting)
   240	                        // Otherwise fall back to the highest overall pin
   241	                        var selectedPin ActionPin
   242	                        if len(compatiblePins) > 0 {
   243	                                selectedPin = compatiblePins[0]
   244	                                actionPinsLog.Printf("No exact match for version %s, using highest semver-compatible version: %s", version, selectedPin.Version)
   245	                        } else {
   246	                                selectedPin = matchingPins[0]
   247	                                actionPinsLog.Printf("No exact match for version %s, no semver-compatible versions found, using highest available: %s", version, selectedPin.Version)
   248	                        }
   249	
   250	                        // Only emit warning if the version is not a SHA (SHAs shouldn't generate warnings)
   251	                        if !isAlreadySHA {
   252	                                // Initialize the warning cache if needed
   253	                                if data.ActionPinWarnings == nil {
   254	                                        data.ActionPinWarnings = make(map[string]bool)
   255	                                }
   256	
   257	                                // Create a cache key for this action@version combination
   258	                                cacheKey := formatActionCacheKey(actionRepo, version)
   259	
   260	                                // Only emit warning if we haven't already warned about this action
   261	                                if !data.ActionPinWarnings[cacheKey] {
   262	                                        warningMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Unable to resolve %s@%s dynamically, using hardcoded pin for %s@%s",
   263	                                                actionRepo, version, actionRepo, selectedPin.Version)
   264	                                        fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(warningMsg))
   265	                                        data.ActionPinWarnings[cacheKey] = true
   266	                                }
   267	                        }
   268	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Using version in non-strict mode: %s@%s (requested) → %s@%s (used)",
   269	                                actionRepo, version, actionRepo, selectedPin.Version)
   270	                        // Use the requested version in the comment, not the pin's version
   271	                        // This preserves the user's intent (e.g., v8 instead of v8.0.0)
   272	                        return formatActionReference(actionRepo, selectedPin.SHA, version), nil
   273	                }
   274	        }
   275	
   276	        // No pin available - emit warning in both strict and non-strict modes
   277	        // Note: This used to fail in strict mode, but it's not always possible to resolve pins
   278	        // so we now emit a warning and continue compilation in both modes
   279	
   280	        // In both strict and non-strict mode, emit warning and return empty string (unless it's already a SHA)
   281	        if isAlreadySHA {
   282	                // If version is already a SHA and we couldn't find it in pins, return it as-is without warnings
   283	                actionPinsLog.Printf("SHA %s not found in hardcoded pins, returning as-is", version)
   284	                return formatActionReference(actionRepo, version, version), nil
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        // Initialize the warning cache if needed
   288	        if data.ActionPinWarnings == nil {
   289	                data.ActionPinWarnings = make(map[string]bool)
   290	        }
   291	
   292	        // Create a cache key for this action@version combination
   293	        cacheKey := formatActionCacheKey(actionRepo, version)
   294	
   295	        // Only emit warning if we haven't already warned about this action
   296	        if !data.ActionPinWarnings[cacheKey] {
   297	                warningMsg := fmt.Sprintf("Unable to pin action %s@%s", actionRepo, version)
   298	                if data.ActionResolver != nil {
   299	                        warningMsg = fmt.Sprintf("Unable to pin action %s@%s: resolution failed", actionRepo, version)
   300	                }
   301	                fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, console.FormatWarningMessage(warningMsg))
   302	                data.ActionPinWarnings[cacheKey] = true
   303	        }
   304	        return "", nil
   305	}
   306	
   307	// ApplyActionPinToTypedStep applies SHA pinning to a WorkflowStep if it uses an action.
   308	// Returns a modified copy of the step with pinned references.
   309	// If the step doesn't use an action or the action is not pinned, returns the original step.
   310	func ApplyActionPinToTypedStep(step *WorkflowStep, data *WorkflowData) *WorkflowStep {
   311	        // Check if step uses an action
   312	        if step == nil || !step.IsUsesStep() {
   313	                return step
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Applying action pin to step: uses=%s", step.Uses)
   317	
   318	        // Extract action repo and version from uses field
   319	        actionRepo := extractActionRepo(step.Uses)
   320	        if actionRepo == "" {
   321	                return step
   322	        }
   323	
   324	        version := extractActionVersion(step.Uses)
   325	        if version == "" {
   326	                // No version specified, can't pin
   327	                return step
   328	        }
   329	
   330	        // Try to get pinned SHA
   331	        pinnedRef, err := GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, version, data)
   332	        if err != nil {
   333	                // In strict mode, this would have already been handled by GetActionPinWithData
   334	                // In normal mode, we just return the original step
   335	                return step
   336	        }
   337	
   338	        if pinnedRef == "" {
   339	                // No pin available for this action, return original step
   340	                return step
   341	        }
   342	
   343	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Pinning action: %s@%s -> %s", actionRepo, version, pinnedRef)
   344	
   345	        // Create a copy of the step with the pinned reference
   346	        result := step.Clone()
   347	        result.Uses = pinnedRef
   348	
   349	        return result
   350	}
   351	
   352	// extractActionRepo extracts the action repository from a uses string
   353	// For example:
   354	//   - "actions/checkout@v5" -> "actions/checkout"
   355	//   - "actions/setup-node@v6" -> "actions/setup-node"
   356	//   - "github/codeql-action/upload-sarif@v3" -> "github/codeql-action/upload-sarif"
   357	//   - "actions/checkout" -> "actions/checkout"
   358	func extractActionRepo(uses string) string {
   359	        // Split on @ to separate repo from version/ref
   360	        before, _, ok := strings.Cut(uses, "@")
   361	        if !ok {
   362	                // No @ found, return the whole string
   363	                return uses
   364	        }
   365	        // Return everything before the @
   366	        return before
   367	}
   368	
   369	// extractActionVersion extracts the version from a uses string
   370	// For example:
   371	//   - "actions/checkout@v5" -> "v4"
   372	//   - "actions/setup-node@v6" -> "v5"
   373	//   - "actions/checkout" -> ""
   374	func extractActionVersion(uses string) string {
   375	        // Split on @ to separate repo from version/ref
   376	        _, after, ok := strings.Cut(uses, "@")
   377	        if !ok {
   378	                // No @ found, no version
   379	                return ""
   380	        }
   381	        // Return everything after the @
   382	        return after
   383	}
   384	
   385	// ApplyActionPinsToTypedSteps applies SHA pinning to a slice of typed WorkflowStep pointers
   386	// Returns a new slice with pinned references - this is the type-safe version
   387	func ApplyActionPinsToTypedSteps(steps []*WorkflowStep, data *WorkflowData) []*WorkflowStep {
   388	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Applying action pins to %d typed steps", len(steps))
   389	        if steps == nil {
   390	                return nil
   391	        }
   392	
   393	        result := make([]*WorkflowStep, 0, len(steps))
   394	        for i, step := range steps {
   395	                if step == nil {
   396	                        actionPinsLog.Printf("Skipping nil step at index %d", i)
   397	                        result = append(result, nil)
   398	                        continue
   399	                }
   400	
   401	                pinnedStep := ApplyActionPinToTypedStep(step, data)
   402	                result = append(result, pinnedStep)
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        actionPinsLog.Printf("Successfully applied pins to %d typed steps", len(result))
   406	        return result
   407	}
   408	
   409	// GetActionPinByRepo returns the ActionPin for a given repository, if it exists
   410	// When multiple versions exist for the same repo, it returns the latest version by semver
   411	func GetActionPinByRepo(repo string) (ActionPin, bool) {
   412	        actionPins := getActionPins()
   413	
   414	        // Find all pins matching the repo - using functional filter
   415	        matchingPins := sliceutil.Filter(actionPins, func(pin ActionPin) bool {
   416	                return pin.Repo == repo
   417	        })
   418	
   419	        if len(matchingPins) == 0 {
   420	                return ActionPin{}, false
   421	        }

    67	// generateMaintenanceCron generates a cron schedule based on the minimum expires value in days
    68	// Schedule runs at minimum required frequency to check expirations at appropriate intervals
    69	// Returns cron expression and description.
    70	func generateMaintenanceCron(minExpiresDays int) (string, string) {
    71	        // Use a pseudo-random but deterministic minute (37) to avoid load spikes at :00
    72	        minute := 37
    73	
    74	        // Determine frequency based on minimum expires value (in days)
    75	        // Run at least as often as the shortest expiration would need
    76	        if minExpiresDays <= 1 {
    77	                // For 1 day or less, run every 2 hours
    78	                return fmt.Sprintf("%d */2 * * *", minute), "Every 2 hours"
    79	        } else if minExpiresDays == 2 {
    80	                // For 2 days, run every 6 hours
    81	                return fmt.Sprintf("%d */6 * * *", minute), "Every 6 hours"
    82	        } else if minExpiresDays <= 4 {
    83	                // For 3-4 days, run every 12 hours
    84	                return fmt.Sprintf("%d */12 * * *", minute), "Every 12 hours"
    85	        }
    86	
    87	        // For more than 4 days, run daily
    88	        return fmt.Sprintf("%d %d * * *", minute, 0), "Daily"
    89	}

    91	// GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow generates the agentics-maintenance.yml workflow
    92	// if any workflows use the expires field for discussions or issues
    93	func GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(workflowDataList []*WorkflowData, workflowDir string, version string, actionMode ActionMode, actionTag string, verbose bool) error {
    94	        maintenanceLog.Print("Checking if maintenance workflow is needed")
    95	
    96	        // Check if any workflow uses expires field for discussions, issues, or pull requests
    97	        // and track the minimum expires value to determine schedule frequency
    98	        hasExpires := false
    99	        minExpires := 0 // Track minimum expires value in hours
   100	
   101	        for _, workflowData := range workflowDataList {
   102	                if workflowData.SafeOutputs != nil {
   103	                        // Check for expired discussions
   104	                        if workflowData.SafeOutputs.CreateDiscussions != nil {

   106	                                        hasExpires = true

   108	                                        maintenanceLog.Printf("Workflow %s has expires field set to %d hours for discussions", workflowData.Name, expires)
   109	                                        if minExpires == 0 || expires < minExpires {
   110	                                                minExpires = expires
   111	                                        }
   112	                                }
   113	                        }
   114	                        // Check for expired issues
   115	                        if workflowData.SafeOutputs.CreateIssues != nil {
   116	                                if workflowData.SafeOutputs.CreateIssues.Expires > 0 {
   117	                                        hasExpires = true
   118	                                        expires := workflowData.SafeOutputs.CreateIssues.Expires
   119	                                        maintenanceLog.Printf("Workflow %s has expires field set to %d hours for issues", workflowData.Name, expires)
   120	                                        if minExpires == 0 || expires < minExpires {
   121	                                                minExpires = expires
   122	                                        }
   123	                                }
   124	                        }
   125	                        // Check for expired pull requests
   126	                        if workflowData.SafeOutputs.CreatePullRequests != nil {
   127	                                if workflowData.SafeOutputs.CreatePullRequests.Expires > 0 {
   128	                                        hasExpires = true

   131	                                        if minExpires == 0 || expires < minExpires {
   132	                                                minExpires = expires
   133	                                        }
   134	                                }
   135	                        }
   136	                }
   137	        }
   138	
   139	        if !hasExpires {
   140	                maintenanceLog.Print("No workflows use expires field, skipping maintenance workflow generation")
   141	
   142	                // Delete existing maintenance workflow file if it exists (no expires means no need for maintenance)
   143	                maintenanceFile := filepath.Join(workflowDir, "agentics-maintenance.yml")

   145	                        maintenanceLog.Printf("Deleting existing maintenance workflow: %s", maintenanceFile)
   146	                        if err := os.Remove(maintenanceFile); err != nil {
   147	                                return fmt.Errorf("failed to delete maintenance workflow: %w", err)
   148	                        }
   149	                        maintenanceLog.Print("Maintenance workflow deleted successfully")
   150	                }
   151	
   152	                return nil
   153	        }
   154	
   155	        maintenanceLog.Printf("Generating maintenance workflow for expired discussions, issues, and pull requests (minimum expires: %d hours)", minExpires)
   156	
   157	        // Convert hours to days for cron schedule generation
   158	        minExpiresDays := minExpires / 24
   159	        if minExpires%24 > 0 {
   160	                minExpiresDays++ // Round up partial days
   161	        }
   162	
   163	        // Generate cron schedule based on minimum expires value
   164	        cronSchedule, scheduleDesc := generateMaintenanceCron(minExpiresDays)
   165	        maintenanceLog.Printf("Maintenance schedule: %s (%s)", cronSchedule, scheduleDesc)
   166	
   167	        // Create the maintenance workflow content using strings.Builder
   168	        var yaml strings.Builder
   169	
   170	        // Add workflow header with logo and instructions
   171	        customInstructions := `Alternative regeneration methods:
   172	  make recompile
   173	
   174	Or use the gh-aw CLI directly:
   175	  ./gh-aw compile --validate --verbose
   176	
   177	The workflow is generated when any workflow uses the 'expires' field
   178	in create-discussions, create-issues, or create-pull-request safe-outputs configuration.
   179	Schedule frequency is automatically determined by the shortest expiration time.`

   192	        description: 'Optional maintenance operation to run'
   193	        required: false

   205	        required: false

   223	        // Use the first available WorkflowData's ActionResolver to enable SHA pinning

    10	var actionRefLog = logger.New("workflow:action_reference")
    11

    14	        GitHubOrgRepo = "github/gh-aw"
    15	
    16	        // GitHubActionsOrgRepo is the organization and repository name for the external gh-aw-actions repository

    20	// ResolveSetupActionReference resolves the actions/setup action reference based on action mode and version.
    21	// This is a standalone helper function that can be used by both Compiler methods and standalone
    22	// workflow generators (like maintenance workflow) that don't have access to WorkflowData.
    23	//
    24	// Parameters:
    25	//   - actionMode: The action mode (dev, release, or action)
    26	//   - version: The version string to use for release/action mode
    27	//   - actionTag: Optional override tag/SHA (takes precedence over version when in release mode)
    28	//   - resolver: Optional ActionSHAResolver for dynamic SHA resolution (can be nil for standalone use)
    29	//
    30	// Returns:
    31	//   - For dev mode: "./actions/setup" (local path)
    32	//   - For release mode with resolver: "github/gh-aw/actions/setup@<sha> # <version>" (SHA-pinned)
    33	//   - For release mode without resolver: "github/gh-aw/actions/setup@<version>" (tag-based, SHA resolved later)
    34	//   - For action mode with resolver: "github/gh-aw-actions/setup@<sha> # <version>" (SHA-pinned)
    35	//   - For action mode without resolver: "github/gh-aw-actions/setup@<version>" (tag-based, SHA resolved later)
    36	//   - Falls back to local path if version is invalid in release/action mode
    37	func ResolveSetupActionReference(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver) string {
    38	        return resolveSetupActionRef(actionMode, version, actionTag, resolver, "")
    39	}
    40	
    41	// resolveSetupActionRef is the internal implementation of ResolveSetupActionReference
    42	// that accepts an optional actionsOrgRepo override. When actionsOrgRepo is empty,
    43	// GitHubActionsOrgRepo is used.
    44	func resolveSetupActionRef(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string, resolver ActionSHAResolver, actionsOrgRepo string) string {
    45	        if actionsOrgRepo == "" {
    46	                actionsOrgRepo = GitHubActionsOrgRepo
    47	        }
    48	
    49	        localPath := "./actions/setup"
    50	
    51	        // Dev mode - return local path
    52	        if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
    53	                actionRefLog.Printf("Dev mode: using local action path: %s", localPath)
    54	                return localPath
    55	        }
    56	
    57	        // Action mode - use external gh-aw-actions repository with SHA pinning if possible
    58	        if actionMode == ActionModeAction {
    59	                // Use actionTag if provided, otherwise fall back to version
    60	                tag := actionTag
    61	                if tag == "" {
    62	                        tag = version
    63	                }
    64	
    65	                // Check if tag is valid for action mode
    66	                if tag == "" || tag == "dev" {
    67	                        actionRefLog.Print("WARNING: No release tag available in binary version (version is 'dev' or empty), falling back to local path")
    68	                        return localPath
    69	                }
    70	
    71	                // Construct the remote reference: <actionsOrgRepo>/setup@tag
    72	                actionRepo := actionsOrgRepo + "/setup"
    73	                remoteRef := fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", actionRepo, tag)
    74	
    75	                // If a resolver is available, try to resolve the SHA
    76	                if resolver != nil {
    77	                        sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, tag)
    78	                        if err == nil && sha != "" {
    79	                                pinnedRef := formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, tag)
    80	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Action mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
    81	                                return pinnedRef
    82	                        }
    83	                        if err != nil {
    84	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, tag, err)
    85	                        }
    86	                }
    87	
    88	                // If no resolver or SHA resolution failed, return tag-based reference
    89	                actionRefLog.Printf("Action mode: using tag-based external actions repo reference: %s (SHA will be resolved later)", remoteRef)
    90	                return remoteRef
    91	        }
    92	
    93	        // Release mode - convert to remote reference
    94	        if actionMode == ActionModeRelease {
    95	                actionPath := strings.TrimPrefix(localPath, "./")
    96	
    97	                // Use actionTag if provided, otherwise fall back to version
    98	                tag := actionTag
    99	                if tag == "" {
   100	                        tag = version
   101	                }
   102	
   103	                // Check if tag is valid for release mode
   104	                if tag == "" || tag == "dev" {
   105	                        actionRefLog.Print("WARNING: No release tag available in binary version (version is 'dev' or empty), falling back to local path")
   106	                        return localPath
   107	                }
   108	
   109	                // Construct the remote reference with tag: github/gh-aw/actions/setup@tag
   110	                actionRepo := fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s", GitHubOrgRepo, actionPath)
   111	                remoteRef := fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", actionRepo, tag)
   112	
   113	                // If a resolver is available, try to resolve the SHA
   114	                if resolver != nil {
   115	                        sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA(actionRepo, tag)
   116	                        if err == nil && sha != "" {
   117	                                pinnedRef := formatActionReference(actionRepo, sha, tag)
   118	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
   119	                                return pinnedRef
   120	                        }
   121	                        if err != nil {
   122	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, tag, err)
   123	                        }
   124	                }
   125	
   126	                // If no resolver or SHA resolution failed, return tag-based reference
   127	                // This is for backward compatibility with standalone workflow generators
   128	                actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: using tag-based remote action reference: %s (SHA will be resolved later)", remoteRef)
   129	                return remoteRef
   130	        }
   131	
   132	        // Unknown mode - default to local path
   133	        actionRefLog.Printf("WARNING: Unknown action mode %s, defaulting to local path", actionMode)
   134	        return localPath
   135	}
   136	
   137	// resolveActionReference converts a local action path to the appropriate reference
   138	// based on the current action mode (dev vs release vs action).
   139	// If action-tag is specified in features, it overrides the mode check and enables action mode behavior
   140	// (using the github/gh-aw-actions external repository).
   141	// For dev mode: returns the local path as-is (e.g., "./actions/create-issue")
   142	// For release mode: converts to SHA-pinned remote reference (e.g., "github/gh-aw/actions/create-issue@SHA # tag")
   143	// For action mode: converts to SHA-pinned reference in external repo if possible (e.g., "github/gh-aw-actions/create-issue@SHA # version")
   144	func (c *Compiler) resolveActionReference(localActionPath string, data *WorkflowData) string {
   145	        // Check if action-tag is specified in features - if so, override mode and use action mode behavior
   146	        hasActionTag := false
   147	        var frontmatterActionTag string
   148	        if data != nil && data.Features != nil {
   149	                if actionTagVal, exists := data.Features["action-tag"]; exists {
   150	                        if actionTagStr, ok := actionTagVal.(string); ok && actionTagStr != "" {
   151	                                hasActionTag = true
   152	                                frontmatterActionTag = actionTagStr
   153	                                actionRefLog.Printf("action-tag feature detected: %s - using action mode behavior", actionTagStr)
   154	                        }
   155	                }
   156	        }
   157	
   158	        // For ./actions/setup, check for compiler-level actionTag override first
   159	        if localActionPath == "./actions/setup" {
   160	                // Use compiler actionTag if available, otherwise check features
   161	                var resolver ActionSHAResolver
   162	                if data != nil && data.ActionResolver != nil {
   163	                        resolver = data.ActionResolver
   164	                }
   165	                if c.actionTag != "" {
   166	                        return resolveSetupActionRef(c.actionMode, c.version, c.actionTag, resolver, c.effectiveActionsRepo())
   167	                }
   168	                if !hasActionTag {
   169	                        return resolveSetupActionRef(c.actionMode, c.version, "", resolver, c.effectiveActionsRepo())
   170	                }
   171	                // hasActionTag is true and no compiler actionTag: use action mode with the frontmatter tag
   172	                return resolveSetupActionRef(ActionModeAction, c.version, frontmatterActionTag, resolver, c.effectiveActionsRepo())
   173	        }
   174	
   175	        // Action mode - use external gh-aw-actions repository
   176	        if c.actionMode == ActionModeAction || hasActionTag {
   177	                return c.convertToExternalActionsRef(localActionPath, data)
   178	        }
   179	
   180	        // Use release mode
   181	        if c.actionMode == ActionModeRelease {
   182	                // Convert to tag-based remote reference for release
   183	                remoteRef := c.convertToRemoteActionRef(localActionPath, data)
   184	                if remoteRef == "" {
   185	                        actionRefLog.Printf("WARNING: Could not resolve remote reference for %s", localActionPath)
   186	                        return ""
   187	                }
   188	
   189	                // Now resolve the tag to a SHA using action pins
   190	                // Extract repo and version from the remote reference (format: "repo/path@version")
   191	                actionRepo := extractActionRepo(remoteRef)
   192	                version := extractActionVersion(remoteRef)
   193	
   194	                if actionRepo != "" && version != "" {
   195	                        // Resolve the SHA using action pins
   196	                        pinnedRef, err := GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, version, data)
   197	                        if err != nil {
   198	                                // In strict mode, GetActionPinWithData returns an error
   199	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Failed to pin action %s@%s: %v", actionRepo, version, err)
   200	                                return ""
   201	                        }
   202	                        if pinnedRef != "" {
   203	                                // Successfully resolved to SHA
   204	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
   205	                                return pinnedRef
   206	                        }
   207	                }
   208	
   209	                // If we couldn't resolve to SHA, return the tag-based reference
   210	                // This happens in non-strict mode when no pin is available
   211	                actionRefLog.Printf("Release mode: using tag-based remote action reference: %s", remoteRef)
   212	                return remoteRef
   213	        }
   214	
   215	        // Dev mode - return local path
   216	        if c.actionMode == ActionModeDev {
   217	                actionRefLog.Printf("Dev mode: using local action path: %s", localActionPath)
   218	                return localActionPath
   219	        }
   220	
   221	        // Default to dev mode for unknown modes
   222	        actionRefLog.Printf("WARNING: Unknown action mode %s, defaulting to dev mode", c.actionMode)
   223	        return localActionPath
   224	}
   225	
   226	// convertToRemoteActionRef converts a local action path to a tag-based remote reference
   227	// that will be resolved to a SHA later in the release pipeline using action pins.
   228	// Uses the action-tag from WorkflowData.Features if specified (for testing), otherwise uses the version stored in the compiler binary.
   229	// If compiler has actionTag set, it takes priority over both.
   230	// Example: "./actions/create-issue" -> "github/gh-aw/actions/create-issue@v1.0.0"
   231	func (c *Compiler) convertToRemoteActionRef(localPath string, data *WorkflowData) string {
   232	        // Strip the leading "./" if present
   233	        actionPath := strings.TrimPrefix(localPath, "./")
   234	
   235	        // Priority order for tag selection:
   236	        // 1. Compiler actionTag (from --action-tag flag)
   237	        // 2. WorkflowData.Features["action-tag"] (from frontmatter)
   238	        // 3. Compiler version
   239	        var tag string
   240	
   241	        // Check compiler actionTag first (highest priority)
   242	        if c.actionTag != "" {
   243	                tag = c.actionTag
   244	                actionRefLog.Printf("Using action-tag from compiler: %s", tag)
   245	        } else if data != nil && data.Features != nil {
   246	                // Check WorkflowData.Features for action-tag
   247	                if actionTagVal, exists := data.Features["action-tag"]; exists {
   248	                        if actionTagStr, ok := actionTagVal.(string); ok && actionTagStr != "" {
   249	                                tag = actionTagStr
   250	                                actionRefLog.Printf("Using action-tag from features: %s", tag)
   251	                        }
   252	                }
   253	        }
   254	
   255	        // Fall back to compiler version if no tag specified
   256	        if tag == "" {
   257	                tag = c.version
   258	                if tag == "" || tag == "dev" {
   259	                        actionRefLog.Print("WARNING: No release tag available in binary version (version is 'dev' or empty)")
   260	                        return ""
   261	                }
   262	                actionRefLog.Printf("Using tag from binary version: %s", tag)
   263	        }
   264	
   265	        // Construct the remote reference with tag: github/gh-aw/actions/name@tag
   266	        // The SHA will be resolved later by action pinning infrastructure
   267	        remoteRef := fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s@%s", GitHubOrgRepo, actionPath, tag)
   268	        actionRefLog.Printf("Remote reference: %s (SHA will be resolved via action pins)", remoteRef)
   269	
   270	        return remoteRef
   271	}
   272	
   273	// convertToExternalActionsRef converts a local action path to a SHA-pinned (if possible) reference
   274	// in the external github/gh-aw-actions repository.
   275	// Example: "./actions/create-issue" -> "github/gh-aw-actions/create-issue@<sha> # v1.0.0"
   276	//
   277	// If SHA resolution fails (no resolver or pin not available), falls back to version-tagged reference:
   278	// Example: "./actions/create-issue" -> "github/gh-aw-actions/create-issue@v1.0.0"
   279	func (c *Compiler) convertToExternalActionsRef(localPath string, data *WorkflowData) string {
   280	        // Strip the leading "./" prefix
   281	        actionPath := strings.TrimPrefix(localPath, "./")
   282	
   283	        // Strip the "actions/" prefix to get just the action name
   284	        // e.g., "actions/create-issue" -> "create-issue"
   285	        actionName := strings.TrimPrefix(actionPath, "actions/")
   286	
   287	        // Determine tag: use compiler actionTag or version
   288	        tag := c.actionTag
   289	        if tag == "" {
   290	                if data != nil && data.Features != nil {
   291	                        if actionTagVal, exists := data.Features["action-tag"]; exists {
   292	                                if actionTagStr, ok := actionTagVal.(string); ok && actionTagStr != "" {
   293	                                        tag = actionTagStr
   294	                                }
   295	                        }
   296	                }
   297	        }
   298	        if tag == "" {
   299	                tag = c.version
   300	                if tag == "" || tag == "dev" {
   301	                        actionRefLog.Print("WARNING: No release tag available in binary version (version is 'dev' or empty)")
   302	                        return ""
   303	                }
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        // Construct the external actions reference: <actionsRepo>/action-name@tag
   307	        actionRepo := fmt.Sprintf("%s/%s", c.effectiveActionsRepo(), actionName)
   308	        remoteRef := fmt.Sprintf("%s@%s", actionRepo, tag)
   309	
   310	        // Try to resolve the SHA using action pins
   311	        if data != nil {
   312	                pinnedRef, err := GetActionPinWithData(actionRepo, tag, data)
   313	                if err != nil {
   314	                        // Log and fall through to tag-based reference (action mode is not strict)
   315	                        actionRefLog.Printf("Failed to pin action %s@%s: %v, falling back to tag-based reference", actionRepo, tag, err)
   316	                } else if pinnedRef != "" {
   317	                        actionRefLog.Printf("Action mode: resolved %s to SHA-pinned reference: %s", remoteRef, pinnedRef)
   318	                        return pinnedRef
   319	                }
   320	        }
   321	
   322	        // If SHA resolution unavailable or pin not found, return tag-based reference
   323	        actionRefLog.Printf("Action mode: using tag-based external actions repo reference: %s (SHA will be resolved later)", remoteRef)
   324	        return remoteRef
   325	}

    12	func TestGenerateMaintenanceCron(t *testing.T) {
    13	        tests := []struct {
    14	                name           string
    15	                minExpiresDays int
    16	                expectedCron   string
    17	                expectedDesc   string
    18	        }{
    19	                {
    20	                        name:           "1 day or less - every 2 hours",
    21	                        minExpiresDays: 1,
    22	                        expectedCron:   "37 */2 * * *",
    23	                        expectedDesc:   "Every 2 hours",
    24	                },
    25	                {
    26	                        name:           "2 days - every 6 hours",
    27	                        minExpiresDays: 2,
    28	                        expectedCron:   "37 */6 * * *",
    29	                        expectedDesc:   "Every 6 hours",
    30	                },
    31	                {
    32	                        name:           "3 days - every 12 hours",
    33	                        minExpiresDays: 3,
    34	                        expectedCron:   "37 */12 * * *",
    35	                        expectedDesc:   "Every 12 hours",
    36	                },
    37	                {
    38	                        name:           "4 days - every 12 hours",
    39	                        minExpiresDays: 4,
    40	                        expectedCron:   "37 */12 * * *",
    41	                        expectedDesc:   "Every 12 hours",
    42	                },
    43	                {
    44	                        name:           "5 days - daily",
    45	                        minExpiresDays: 5,
    46	                        expectedCron:   "37 0 * * *",
    47	                        expectedDesc:   "Daily",
    48	                },
    49	                {
    50	                        name:           "7 days - daily",
    51	                        minExpiresDays: 7,
    52	                        expectedCron:   "37 0 * * *",
    53	                        expectedDesc:   "Daily",
    54	                },
    55	                {
    56	                        name:           "30 days - daily",
    57	                        minExpiresDays: 30,
    58	                        expectedCron:   "37 0 * * *",
    59	                        expectedDesc:   "Daily",
    60	                },
    61	        }
    62	
    63	        for _, tt := range tests {
    64	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
    65	                        cron, desc := generateMaintenanceCron(tt.minExpiresDays)
    66	                        if cron != tt.expectedCron {
    67	                                t.Errorf("generateMaintenanceCron(%d) cron = %q, expected %q", tt.minExpiresDays, cron, tt.expectedCron)
    68	                        }
    69	                        if desc != tt.expectedDesc {
    70	                                t.Errorf("generateMaintenanceCron(%d) desc = %q, expected %q", tt.minExpiresDays, desc, tt.expectedDesc)
    71	                        }
    72	                })
    73	        }
    74	}

    76	func TestGenerateMaintenanceWorkflow_WithExpires(t *testing.T) {
    77	        tests := []struct {
    78	                name                    string
    79	                workflowDataList        []*WorkflowData
    80	                expectWorkflowGenerated bool
    81	                expectError             bool
    82	        }{
    83	                {
    84	                        name: "with expires in discussions - should generate workflow",
    85	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
    86	                                {
    87	                                        Name: "test-workflow",
    88	                                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
    89	                                                CreateDiscussions: &CreateDiscussionsConfig{
    90	                                                        Expires: 168, // 7 days
    91	                                                },
    92	                                        },
    93	                                },
    94	                        },
    95	                        expectWorkflowGenerated: true,
    96	                        expectError:             false,
    97	                },
    98	                {
    99	                        name: "with expires in issues - should generate workflow",
   100	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
   101	                                {
   102	                                        Name: "test-workflow-issues",
   103	                                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
   104	                                                CreateIssues: &CreateIssuesConfig{
   105	                                                        Expires: 48, // 2 days
   106	                                                },
   107	                                        },
   108	                                },
   109	                        },
   110	                        expectWorkflowGenerated: true,
   111	                        expectError:             false,
   112	                },
   113	                {
   114	                        name: "without expires field - should NOT generate workflow",
   115	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
   116	                                {
   117	                                        Name: "test-workflow",
   118	                                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
   119	                                                CreateDiscussions: &CreateDiscussionsConfig{},
   120	                                        },
   121	                                },
   122	                        },
   123	                        expectWorkflowGenerated: false,
   124	                        expectError:             false,
   125	                },
   126	                {
   127	                        name: "with both discussions and issues expires - should generate workflow",
   128	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
   129	                                {
   130	                                        Name: "multi-expires-workflow",
   131	                                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
   132	                                                CreateDiscussions: &CreateDiscussionsConfig{
   133	                                                        Expires: 168,
   134	                                                },
   135	                                                CreateIssues: &CreateIssuesConfig{
   136	                                                        Expires: 48,
   137	                                                },
   138	                                        },
   139	                                },
   140	                        },
   141	                        expectWorkflowGenerated: true,
   142	                        expectError:             false,
   143	                },
   144	        }
   145	
   146	        for _, tt := range tests {
   147	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   148	                        // Create a temporary directory for the workflow
   149	                        tmpDir := t.TempDir()
   150	
   151	                        // Call GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow
   152	                        err := GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(tt.workflowDataList, tmpDir, "v1.0.0", ActionModeDev, "", false)
   153	
   154	                        // Check error expectation
   155	                        if tt.expectError && err == nil {
   156	                                t.Errorf("Expected error but got none")
   157	                        }
   158	                        if !tt.expectError && err != nil {
   159	                                t.Errorf("Unexpected error: %v", err)
   160	                        }
   161	
   162	                        // Check if workflow file was generated
   163	                        maintenanceFile := filepath.Join(tmpDir, "agentics-maintenance.yml")
   164	                        _, statErr := os.Stat(maintenanceFile)
   165	                        workflowExists := statErr == nil
   166	
   167	                        if tt.expectWorkflowGenerated && !workflowExists {
   168	                                t.Errorf("Expected maintenance workflow to be generated but it was not")
   169	                        }

   171	                                t.Errorf("Expected maintenance workflow NOT to be generated but it was")
   172	                        }
   173	                })
   174	        }

   177	func TestGenerateMaintenanceWorkflow_DeletesExistingFile(t *testing.T) {
   178	        tests := []struct {
   179	                name             string
   180	                workflowDataList []*WorkflowData
   181	                createFileBefore bool
   182	                expectFileExists bool
   183	        }{
   184	                {
   185	                        name: "no expires field - should delete existing file",
   186	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
   187	                                {
   188	                                        Name: "test-workflow",

   190	                                                CreateDiscussions: &CreateDiscussionsConfig{},
   191	                                        },
   192	                                },
   193	                        },
   194	                        createFileBefore: true,
   195	                        expectFileExists: false,
   196	                },
   197	                {
   198	                        name: "with expires - should create file",
   199	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
   200	                                {
   201	                                        Name: "test-workflow",
   202	                                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
   203	                                                CreateDiscussions: &CreateDiscussionsConfig{
   204	                                                        Expires: 168,
   205	                                                },
   206	                                        },
   207	                                },
   208	                        },
   209	                        createFileBefore: false,
   210	                        expectFileExists: true,
   211	                },
   212	                {
   213	                        name: "no expires without existing file - should not error",
   214	                        workflowDataList: []*WorkflowData{
   215	                                {
   216	                                        Name: "test-workflow",
   217	                                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
   218	                                                CreateDiscussions: &CreateDiscussionsConfig{},
   219	                                        },
   220	                                },
   221	                        },
   222	                        createFileBefore: false,
   223	                        expectFileExists: false,
   224	                },
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        for _, tt := range tests {
   228	                t.Run(tt.name, func(t *testing.T) {

   230	                        maintenanceFile := filepath.Join(tmpDir, "agentics-maintenance.yml")

   236	                                        t.Fatalf("Failed to create test file: %v", err)
   237	                                }
   238	                        }
   239	
   240	                        // Call GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow
   241	                        err := GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(tt.workflowDataList, tmpDir, "v1.0.0", ActionModeDev, "", false)

   243	                                t.Errorf("Unexpected error: %v", err)
   244	                        }

   246	                        // Check if file exists
   247	                        _, statErr := os.Stat(maintenanceFile)
   248	                        fileExists := statErr == nil
   249	
   250	                        if tt.expectFileExists && !fileExists {
   251	                                t.Errorf("Expected maintenance workflow file to exist but it does not")
   252	                        }
   253	                        if !tt.expectFileExists && fileExists {
   254	                                t.Errorf("Expected maintenance workflow file NOT to exist but it does")
   255	                        }

   260	func TestGenerateMaintenanceWorkflow_OperationJobConditions(t *testing.T) {
   261	        workflowDataList := []*WorkflowData{
   262	                {
   263	                        Name: "test-workflow",
   264	                        SafeOutputs: &SafeOutputsConfig{
   265	                                CreateIssues: &CreateIssuesConfig{
   266	                                        Expires: 48,
   267	                                },
   268	                        },
   269	                },
   270	        }
   271	
   272	        tmpDir := t.TempDir()
   273	        err := GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(workflowDataList, tmpDir, "v1.0.0", ActionModeDev, "", false)
   274	        if err != nil {
   275	                t.Fatalf("Unexpected error: %v", err)
   276	        }
   277	        content, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join(tmpDir, "agentics-maintenance.yml"))
   278	        if err != nil {
   279	                t.Fatalf("Expected maintenance workflow to be generated: %v", err)
   280	        }
   281	        yaml := string(content)
   282	
   283	        operationSkipCondition := `github.event_name != 'workflow_dispatch' || github.event.inputs.operation == ''`
   284	        operationRunCondition := `github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' && github.event.inputs.operation != '' && github.event.inputs.operation != 'safe_outputs'`
   285	        applySafeOutputsCondition := `github.event_name == 'workflow_dispatch' && github.event.inputs.operation == 'safe_outputs'`
   286	
   287	        const jobSectionSearchRange = 300
   288	        const runOpSectionSearchRange = 200
   289	
   290	        // Jobs that should be disabled when operation is set
   291	        disabledJobs := []string{"close-expired-entities:", "compile-workflows:", "zizmor-scan:", "secret-validation:"}
   292	        for _, job := range disabledJobs {
   293	                // Find the if: condition for each job
   294	                jobIdx := strings.Index(yaml, "\n  "+job)
   295	                if jobIdx == -1 {
   296	                        t.Errorf("Job %q not found in generated workflow", job)
   297	                        continue
   298	                }
   299	                // Check that the operation skip condition appears after the job name (within a reasonable range)
   300	                jobSection := yaml[jobIdx : jobIdx+jobSectionSearchRange]
   301	                if !strings.Contains(jobSection, operationSkipCondition) {
   302	                        t.Errorf("Job %q is missing the operation skip condition %q in:\n%s", job, operationSkipCondition, jobSection)
   303	                }
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        // run_operation job should NOT have the skip condition but should have its own activation condition
   307	        // and should exclude safe_outputs
   308	        runOpIdx := strings.Index(yaml, "\n  run_operation:")
   309	        if runOpIdx == -1 {
   310	                t.Errorf("Job run_operation not found in generated workflow")
   311	        } else {
   312	                runOpSection := yaml[runOpIdx : runOpIdx+runOpSectionSearchRange]
   313	                if strings.Contains(runOpSection, operationSkipCondition) {
   314	                        t.Errorf("Job run_operation should NOT have the operation skip condition")
   315	                }
   316	                if !strings.Contains(runOpSection, operationRunCondition) {
   317	                        t.Errorf("Job run_operation should have the activation condition %q", operationRunCondition)
   318	                }
   319	        }
   320	
   321	        // apply_safe_outputs job should be triggered when operation == 'safe_outputs'
   322	        applyIdx := strings.Index(yaml, "\n  apply_safe_outputs:")
   323	        if applyIdx == -1 {
   324	                t.Errorf("Job apply_safe_outputs not found in generated workflow")
   325	        } else {
   326	                applySection := yaml[applyIdx : applyIdx+runOpSectionSearchRange]
   327	                if !strings.Contains(applySection, applySafeOutputsCondition) {
   328	                        t.Errorf("Job apply_safe_outputs should have the activation condition %q in:\n%s", applySafeOutputsCondition, applySection)
   329	                }
   330	        }
   331	
   332	        // Verify safe_outputs is an option in the operation choices
   333	        if !strings.Contains(yaml, "- 'safe_outputs'") {
   334	                t.Error("workflow_dispatch operation choices should include 'safe_outputs'")
   335	        }
   336	
   337	        // Verify run_url input exists in workflow_dispatch
   338	        if !strings.Contains(yaml, "run_url:") {
   339	                t.Error("workflow_dispatch should include run_url input")
   340	        }
   341	}

   360	                }

   362	                if err != nil {
   363	                        t.Fatalf("Expected maintenance workflow to be generated: %v", err)
   364	                }
   365	                if !strings.Contains(string(content), "github/gh-aw/actions/setup@v0.47.4") {
   366	                        t.Errorf("Expected remote ref with action-tag v0.47.4, got:\n%s", string(content))
   367	                }
   368	                if strings.Contains(string(content), "uses: ./actions/setup") {
   369	                        t.Errorf("Expected no local path in release mode with action-tag, got:\n%s", string(content))
   370	                }
   371	        })
   372	
   373	        t.Run("release mode with action-tag and resolver uses SHA-pinned ref", func(t *testing.T) {
   374	                tmpDir := t.TempDir()
   375	                // Set up an action resolver with a cached SHA for the setup action
   376	                cache := NewActionCache(tmpDir)
   377	                cache.Set("github/gh-aw/actions/setup", "v0.47.4", "aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa")
   378	                resolver := NewActionResolver(cache)
   379	
   380	                workflowDataListWithResolver := []*WorkflowData{
   381	                        {

   386	                                        CreateIssues: &CreateIssuesConfig{
   387	                                                Expires: 48,
   388	                                        },
   389	                                },
   390	                        },
   391	                }
   392	
   393	                err := GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(workflowDataListWithResolver, tmpDir, "v1.0.0", ActionModeRelease, "v0.47.4", false)
   394	                if err != nil {
   395	                        t.Fatalf("Unexpected error: %v", err)
   396	                }
   397	                content, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join(tmpDir, "agentics-maintenance.yml"))
   398	                if err != nil {
   399	                        t.Fatalf("Expected maintenance workflow to be generated: %v", err)
   400	                }
   401	                expectedRef := "github/gh-aw/actions/setup@aaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaaa # v0.47.4"
   402	                if !strings.Contains(string(content), expectedRef) {
   403	                        t.Errorf("Expected SHA-pinned ref %q, got:\n%s", expectedRef, string(content))
   404	                }
   405	                if strings.Contains(string(content), "uses: ./actions/setup") {
   406	                        t.Errorf("Expected no local path in release mode with action-tag, got:\n%s", string(content))
   407	                }
   408	        })
   409	
   410	        t.Run("dev mode ignores action-tag and uses local path", func(t *testing.T) {
   411	                tmpDir := t.TempDir()
   412	                err := GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow(workflowDataList, tmpDir, "v1.0.0", ActionModeDev, "v0.47.4", false)
   413	                if err != nil {
   414	                        t.Fatalf("Unexpected error: %v", err)
   415	                }
   416	                content, err := os.ReadFile(filepath.Join(tmpDir, "agentics-maintenance.yml"))
   417	                if err != nil {
   418	                        t.Fatalf("Expected maintenance workflow to be generated: %v", err)
   419	                }
   420	                if !strings.Contains(string(content), "uses: ./actions/setup") {
   421	                        t.Errorf("Expected local path in dev mode, got:\n%s", string(content))
   422	                }
   423	        })
   424	}

   456	                        t.Errorf("Release mode should use actionTag v2.0.0, got:\n%s", result)

   458	        })

    13	)
    14	
    15	var copilotSetupLog = logger.New("cli:copilot_setup")
    16	
    17	// getActionRef returns the action reference string based on action mode and version.
    18	// If a resolver is provided and mode is release or action, attempts to resolve the SHA for a SHA-pinned reference.
    19	// Falls back to a version tag reference if SHA resolution fails or resolver is nil.
    20	func getActionRef(actionMode workflow.ActionMode, version string, resolver workflow.ActionSHAResolver) string {
    21	        if actionMode.IsRelease() && version != "" && version != "dev" {
    22	                if resolver != nil {
    23	                        sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA("github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli", version)
    24	                        if err == nil && sha != "" {
    25	                                return fmt.Sprintf("@%s # %s", sha, version)
    26	                        }
    27	                        copilotSetupLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for setup-cli@%s: %v, falling back to version tag", version, err)
    28	                }
    29	                return "@" + version
    30	        }
    31	        if actionMode.IsAction() && version != "" && version != "dev" {
    32	                if resolver != nil {
    33	                        sha, err := resolver.ResolveSHA("github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli", version)
    34	                        if err == nil && sha != "" {
    35	                                return fmt.Sprintf("@%s # %s", sha, version)
    36	                        }
    37	                        copilotSetupLog.Printf("Failed to resolve SHA for gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@%s: %v, falling back to version tag", version, err)
    38	                }
    39	                return "@" + version

    15	// generateInstallCLISteps generates YAML steps to install or build the gh-aw CLI.
    16	// In dev mode: builds from source using Setup Go + Build gh-aw (./gh-aw binary available)
    17	// In release mode: installs the released CLI via the setup-cli action (gh aw available)
    18	// In action mode: installs the released CLI via the gh-aw-actions/setup-cli action (gh aw available)
    19	func generateInstallCLISteps(actionMode ActionMode, version string, actionTag string) string {
    20	        if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
    21	                return `      - name: Setup Go
    22	        uses: ` + GetActionPin("actions/setup-go") + `
    23	        with:
    24	          go-version-file: go.mod
    25	          cache: true
    26	
    27	      - name: Build gh-aw
    28	        run: make build
    29	
    30	`
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        cliTag := actionTag
    34	        if cliTag == "" {
    35	                cliTag = version
    36	        }
    37	
    38	        // Action mode: use setup-cli action from external gh-aw-actions repository
    39	        if actionMode == ActionModeAction {
    40	                return `      - name: Install gh-aw
    41	        uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@` + cliTag + `
    42	        with:
    43	          version: ` + cliTag + `
    44	
    45	`
    46	        }
    47	
    48	        // Release mode: use setup-cli action (consistent with copilot-setup-steps.yml)
    49	        return `      - name: Install gh-aw
    50	        uses: github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli@` + cliTag + `
    51	        with:
    52	          version: ` + cliTag + `
    53	
    54	`
    55	}

Now I can see the full picture. The `GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow` has access to a resolver (line 224-228), which is used for `ResolveSetupActionReference` for the "setup" action. But the `generateInstallCLISteps` function that generates the "setup-cli" references does NOT use the resolver or `GetActionPin()`.

The fix should:

1. Modify `generateInstallCLISteps` to accept a resolver parameter and use SHA pinning for the `setup-cli` action references
2. Add the `setup-cli` action pins to `action_pins.json`

But wait - looking at the PR description more carefully, it says:
- "The compiler's action pinning logic (via `GetActionPin()` and `.github/aw/actions-lock.json`) did not resolve and emit the commit SHA for `setup-cli`"
- "Ensure `GetActionPin()` (or equivalent) correctly resolves and emits the SHA for `setup-cli` in all compiler code paths, including maintenance workflow generation."

So the fix is two-fold:
1. Add `setup-cli` related entries to `action_pins.json`
2. Modify `generateInstallCLISteps` to use `GetActionPin()` or `GetActionPinWithData()` for SHA pinning

But note that `GetActionPin` only takes a repo (no version), and returns the latest version. `GetActionPinWithData` takes repo, version, and data. Since `generateInstallCLISteps` doesn't have access to `WorkflowData`, we need to either:
- Use `GetActionPin` (which uses the latest version)
- Change the function signature to accept data/resolver

Let me look at how this is called and if we can pass the resolver:

Looking at line 315 and 402, `generateInstallCLISteps` is called with `(actionMode, version, actionTag)`. The resolver is available in `GenerateMaintenanceWorkflow` at line 224-228.

package main

import (
    "fmt"
    "strings"
)

func main() {
    // Simulate what generateInstallCLISteps outputs for action mode
    cliTag := "v0.64.0"
    actionMode := "action"
    
    if actionMode == "action" {
        result := "uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@" + cliTag
        fmt.Println("Action mode output:")
        fmt.Println(result)
        
        // Check if it's SHA-pinned
        if strings.Contains(result, "@"+cliTag) && !strings.Contains(result, " # ") {
            fmt.Println("BUG: Not SHA-pinned! Uses mutable tag:", cliTag)
        }
    }
    
    // Release mode
    result := "uses: github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli@" + cliTag
    fmt.Println("\nRelease mode output:")
    fmt.Println(result)
    
    if strings.Contains(result, "@"+cliTag) && !strings.Contains(result, " # ") {
        fmt.Println("BUG: Not SHA-pinned! Uses mutable tag:", cliTag)
    }
}

Let me re-read the PR description: "BUG: 'setup-cli' action referenced by mutable tag instead of commit SHA in maintenance workflow". The issue is specifically about the maintenance workflow.

Let me think about the minimal fix:

The core issue is in `generateInstallCLISteps` which outputs:
- `uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@<cliTag>` (action mode)
- `uses: github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli@<cliTag>` (release mode)

Instead, it should output SHA-pinned references like:
- `uses: github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli@<sha> # <cliTag>`

The simplest fix is to:
1. Add the `setup-cli` pins to `action_pins.json`
2. Modify `generateInstallCLISteps` to use `GetActionPin` for the appropriate repo

But `GetActionPin` returns the latest version, not a specific one. The `cliTag` could be any version. If we always use `GetActionPin`, we might get a different version than requested.

However, looking at the existing usage pattern in `maintenance_workflow.go`:
- Line 22: `GetActionPin("actions/setup-go")` - always gets latest
- Line 233: `GetActionPin("actions/checkout")` - always gets latest

So the pattern is to always use the latest version. For `setup-cli`, the same pattern should apply.

But wait, there's a nuance: the `cliTag` and `version` parameters are used not just for the `uses:` reference but also for the `version:` input parameter. The `version:` input tells the `setup-cli` action which version of the CLI to install. That should probably remain as the requested version (not the latest pinned version).

Let me now implement the changes

Looking at the function:
- In release mode, it uses `github/gh-aw/actions/setup-cli`
- In action mode, it uses `github/gh-aw-actions/setup-cli`

The function needs to:
1. Use `GetActionPin` for the appropriate repo to get the SHA-pinned reference
2. If `GetActionPin` returns empty (no pin found), fall back to using the tag

Let me also consider that `GetActionPin` returns the latest version, but the `version` input to the action should still use `cliTag` (the requested version to install).

	if actionMode == ActionModeDev {
		return `      - name: Setup Go
        uses: ` + GetActionPin("actions/setup-go") + `
        with:
          go-version-file: go.mod
          cache: true

      - name: Build gh-aw
        run: make build

`
	}

	if cliTag == "" {
